the distance between the two lines.	Izmjerite udaljenost između dvije oznake na tlu.	english-croatian

applied when exercising.	Ova funkcija je jako korisna ako uvijek	english-croatian

environment. If automatic calibration fails, you are not in the usual environment and will need to calibrate	Ako automatska kalibracija ne uspije, niste u uobičajenoj	english-croatian
the altitude manually.	okolini i morati ćete nadmorsku visinu kalibrirati ručno.	english-croatian
Altitude calibrated to xx m/ft indicates that calibration has succeeded.	Altitude calibrated to xx m/ft označava da je kalibracija uspjela.	english-croatian
If Altitude calibration failed is	Ako se prikaže Altitude calibration	english-croatian
displayed, re-calibrate the altitude.	failed , ponovo kalibrirajte nadmorsku visinu.	english-croatian
Recording Rate	Učestalost snimanja	english-croatian
Select Settings > Features > Rec.rate > 1 / 2 / 5 / 15 / 60 sec	Odaberite Settings > Features > Rec.rate > 1 / 2 / 5 / 15 / 60 sec	english-croatian
The training computer can store your heart rate, speed/pace,* and altitude in 1, 2, 5, 15 or 60 second intervals.	Monitor srčane frekvencije može spremiti vaše otkucaje srca, brzinu, ritam* i nadmorsku visinu u intervalima od 1,2 ,5, 15 ili 60 sekundi.	english-croatian
A longer interval gives you more recording time, while a shorter interval allows you to record	Duži interval omogućuje duže vrijeme snimanja, dok kraći interval	english-croatian
more heart and other data.	omogućuje snimanje više podataka.	english-croatian
This enables accurate data analysis using the software.	To omogućuje preciznu analizu podataka koristeći softver.	english-croatian
A shorter recording rate consumes the memory of the training computer more rapidly.	Kraći interval snimanja brže troši memoriju monitora srčane frekvencije.	english-croatian
The remaining	Prilikom namještanja intervala u	english-croatian
recording time is displayed on the lower row when setting the rate.	donjem redu se prikazuje preostalo vrijeme snimanja.	english-croatian
Default recording rate is 5 seconds.	Standardni interval je 5 sekundi.	english-croatian
When less than 30 minutes of maximum recording time is left, the recording rate changes automatically to	Kada ostane manje od 30 minuta maksimalnog vremena za snimanje, interval snimanja se automatski	english-croatian
longer recording time (1s > 2s > 5s > 15s > 60s).	prebacuje na duži interval (1s > 2s > 5s > 15s > 60s).	english-croatian
This will maximize the time to record exercise data.	To će maksimalizirati vrijeme snimanja podataka o	english-croatian
When the session ends, the current recording rate remains as default.	vježbanju. Kada ciklus završi, u slijedećem intervalu vježbanja će se koristiti trenutni interval snimanja.	english-croatian
The following table shows the maximum recording times for each recording rate.	Slijedeća tablica prikazuje maksimalna vremena snimanja za svaki interval snimanja.	english-croatian
Note that recording rate	Uzmite u obzir da	english-croatian
might change when there is less than 30 minutes of recording time left.	se učestalost snimanja može promijeniti kad ostane manje od 30 minuta za snimanje.	english-croatian

9. TESTS	9. TESTOVI	english-croatian
Polar Fitness Test TM	Polar Fitness Test TM	english-croatian
The Polar Fitness Test TM is an easy, safe, and quick way to measure your aerobic (cardiovascular) fitness	Polar Fitness Test TM je lak, siguran i brz način za mjerenje vaših aerobnih (kardiovaskularnih)	english-croatian
at rest.	sposobnosti u mirovanju.	english-croatian
The result, Polar OwnIndex, is comparable to maximal oxygen uptake (VO2max), which is commonly	Rezultat, Polar OwnIndex, je usporediv s maksimalnim unosom kisika (VO 2max),	english-croatian
used to evaluate aerobic fitness.	koji se obično koristi za ocjenu aerobnih sposobnosti.	english-croatian
Your long-term level of physical activity, heart rate, heart rate variability	Vaša dugoročna fizička aktivnost, otkucaji srca,	english-croatian
at rest, gender, age, height, and body weight all influence OwnIndex.	promjenjivost otkucaja srca u mirovanju, spol, starost, visina i masa utječu na OwnIndex.	english-croatian
The Polar Fitness Test is developed	Polar Fitness Test je razvijen da ga koriste zdrave odrasle osobe.	english-croatian
	Aerobna sposobnost se odnosi na činjenicu koliko dobro vaš kardiovaskularni sustav radi za prijenos	english-croatian
for use by healthy adults.	kisika u vaše tijelo.	english-croatian
Aerobic fitness relates to how well your cardiovascular system works to transport oxygen to your body.	Što imate više aerobne sposobnosti, to je vaše srce jače i efikasnije.	english-croatian
The	Dobre aerobne	english-croatian
better your aerobic fitness, the stronger and more efficient your heart is.	sposobnosti imaju mnoge zdravstvene prednosti.	english-croatian
Good aerobic fitness has many health benefits.	Na primjer, pomažu u smanjenju visokog krvnog tlaka i	english-croatian
For example, it helps in decreasing high blood pressure and your risk of cardiovascular	rizika od kardiovaskularnih bolesti i srčanog udara.	english-croatian
diseases and stroke.	Ako želite poboljšati vaše aerobne sposobnosti, u	english-croatian
If you want to improve your aerobic fitness it takes, on average, six weeks of regular	prosjeku treba šest tjedana redovitog vježbanja kako bi vidjeli značajnu promjenu vašeg OwnIndexa.	english-croatian
training to see a noticeable change in your OwnIndex.	Manje sposobni pojedinci će brže uočiti promjene.	english-croatian
Less fit individuals see progress even more rapidly.	Što su vaše aerobne sposobnosti veće, to će	english-croatian
The better your aerobic fitness, the smaller the improvements in your OwnIndex.	promjene vašeg OwnIndexa biti manje	english-croatian
Aerobic fitness is best improved by exercise types that use large muscle groups.	Aerobne sposobnosti se najbolje poboljšavaju vrstama vježbi koje koriste velike grupe mišića.	english-croatian

Determining Maximum Heart Rate	vježbanja.	english-croatian
Your HR max can be determined in several ways.	Određivanje maksimalnog broja otkucaja srca	english-croatian
• The most accurate way is to have your HRmax clinically measured, usually on a maximal treadmill or by		english-croatian
taking a bicycle stress test supervised by a cardiologist or exercise physiologist.		english-croatian
• You can also determine your HR max by taking a field test together with a training partner.	Vaš HR max se može odrediti na nekoliko načina.	english-croatian
• You can obtain a HR max-p score that predicts your HRmax by taking a Polar Fitness Test.	• Najtočniji način je kliničko mjerenje HR max vrijednosti.	english-croatian
• HRmax can also be estimated by using the commonly used formula: 220 - age, although research shows	Test stresa koji nadzire kardiolog ili fiziolog	english-croatian
that the method is not very accurate, especially for older persons or those who have been fit for many	vježbanja se obično provodi na traci za trčanje ili biciklu.	english-croatian

Here is an example of a simple test.	Ovdje je dan primjer jednostavnog testa.	english-croatian
Step 1: Warm up for 15 minutes on a flat surface, building up to your usual training pace.	Step 1: Zagrijavajte se 15 minuta na ravnoj površini, postepeno se približavajući vaše uobičajenom ritmu vježbanja.	english-croatian
Step 2: Choose a hill or stairwell that will take more than 2 minutes to climb.	Step 2: Odaberite uspon ili stepenište, za koji će vam trebati više od 2 minute da ga svladate.	english-croatian
Run up the hill/steps once,	Potrčite uz	english-croatian
building to as hard a pace as you can hold for 20 minutes.	brdo/stepenište, održavajući što je veći ritam koji možete izdržati 20 minuta.	english-croatian
Return to the base of the hill/steps.	Vratite se u podnožje uspona.	english-croatian
Step 3: Run up the hill/steps again, building towards a pace you could just about hold for 3 kilometers.	Step 3: Ponovo potrčite uz brdo, približavajući se ritmu koji bi mogli izdržati 3 kilometra. Zabilježite vaš	english-croatian
Note your highest heart rate.	najviši broj otkucaja srca.	english-croatian
Your maximum is approximately 10 beats higher than the noted value.	Vaš maksimum je otprilike 10 otkucaja viši od zabilježene vrijednosti.	english-croatian
Step 4: Run back down the hill, allowing your heart rate to drop 30-40 beats per minute.	Step 4: Otrčite nazad niz brdo, dopuštajući da vam broj otkucaja srca padne za 30-40 otkucaja u minuti.	english-croatian
Step 5: Run up the hill/steps once again at a pace that you can only hold for 1 minute.	Step 5: Ponovo potrčite uz brdo ritmom koji bi mogli izdržati 1 minutu.	english-croatian
Try to run halfway	Pokušajte trčati do polovice	english-croatian
up the hills/steps.	uspona.	english-croatian
Note your highest heart rate.	Zabilježite vaš najviši broj otkucaja srca.	english-croatian
This brings you close to your maximum heart rate.	To vas dovodi do vašeg maksimalnog broja otkucaja	english-croatian
Use this	srca.	english-croatian

Heart Rate Value in a Sitting Position	Otkucaji srca u sjedećem položaju	english-croatian
HRsit is your average heart rate when completely still (i.e. while sitting).	HRsit predstavlja prosječni broj otkucaja srca kada potpuno mirujete (odnosno sjedite).	english-croatian
To easily determine HR sit, wear your heart rate sensor, sit down, and do not engage in any physical activity.	Za lako određivanje HR sit, nosite vaš primopredajnik, sjednite i ne radite nikakvu fizičku aktivnost.	english-croatian
For a more precise	Za preciznije	english-croatian
measurement, repeat the procedure several times and calculate your average.	mjerenje, ponovite postupak nekoliko puta i izračunajte prosječnu vrijednost.	english-croatian
Heart Rate Reserve	Rezerva otkucaja srca	english-croatian
Heart rate reserve (HRR) is the difference between maximum heart rate (HRmax), and resting heart rate	Rezerva otkucaja srca (HRR) je razlika između maksimalnog broja otkucaja srca (HR max) i otkucaja srca	english-croatian
(HRrest)*.	u mirovanju (HR rest)*.	english-croatian
HRR is used to calculate exercise heart rates.	HRR se koristi za proračun otkucaja srca prilikom vježbanja.	english-croatian
It is the range within which heart rate varies	To je raspon u kojem	english-croatian
depending on exertion level.	se mijenja broj otkucaja srca ovisno o razini napora.	english-croatian
HRR equals oxygen uptake reserve (VO2R).	HRR odgovara rezervi unosa kisika (VO 2R).	english-croatian
Exercise heart rate can be determined by using the Karvonen formula**.	Otkucaji srca tijekom vježbanja se mogu odrediti koristeći Karvonen formulu**.	english-croatian
Add the given percentage of heart	Dodajte dani postotak	english-croatian
rate reserve to resting heart rate.	rezerve otkucaja srca otkucajima srca u mirovanju.	english-croatian
Exercise HR = % of target intensity (HRmax – HRrest) + HRrest	HR vježbanje = % ciljanog intenziteta (HR max – HRrest) + HRrest	english-croatian
Example:	Primjer:	english-croatian
Target intensity 70 % HRR for a person with HR max 201 bpm and HRrest 50 bpm	Ciljani intenzitet je 70% HRR za osobu s HR max 201 bpm and HR rest 50 bpm	english-croatian
Exercise HR= 70% (201-50) + 50	HR vježbanje = 70% (201-50) + 50	english-croatian
Exercise HR=156 bpm	HR vježbanje = 156 bpm	english-croatian
For a precise exercise heart rate, you need your exact HRmax and HRrest.	Za precizni broj otkucaja srca tijekom vježbanja, trebate vaše točne vrijednosti HR max i HRrest.	english-croatian
When using estimated HRmax,	To je zbog	english-croatian
exercise heart rate values are always estimates.	praktičnih razloga jer se HRmax otkucaji srca tijekom vježbanja su uvijek procijenjeni.	english-croatian
*In Polar RS800CX training computer, the heart rate value during a resting state is measured in a sitting	*Kod monitora srčane frekvencije RS800CX, vrijednost otkucaja srca za vrijeme odmaranja se mjeri u	english-croatian
position (HRsit).	sjedećem položaju (HRsit).	english-croatian
This is for practical reasons since HRsit is used in energy expenditure calculation because of accuracy.		english-croatian
HR sit matches the low intensity to which different exercise intensities can be compared.	To je zbog praktičnih razloga jer se HR sit koristi u proračunu potrošnje	english-croatian
**Karvonen M, Kentala K, Mustala O. The effects of training on heart rate: a longitudinal study. Ann Med		english-croatian
Exp Biol Fenn 1957; 35: 307-315.		english-croatian
Heart Rate Variability	energije zbog točnosti.	english-croatian
Heart rate varies with every heartbeat. Heart rate variability (HRV) is the variation of beat to beat intervals,	HR sit odgovara niskom intenzitetu s kojim se mogu usporediti različiti intenziteti	english-croatian
also known as R-R intervals.	vježbanja.	english-croatian

HRV indicates the fluctuations of heart rate around an average heart rate.	**Karvonen M. Kentala K, Mustala O. The effects of training on heart rate: a longitudinal study, Med Exp	english-croatian
An average heart rate of 60	Biol Fenn 1957; 35:307-315.	english-croatian
	Promjenjivost otkucaja srca	english-croatian
beats per minute (bpm) does not mean that the interval between successive heartbeats would be exactly	Broj otkucaja srca se mijenja sa svakim otkucajem. Promjenjivost otkucaja srca (HRV) je promjena	english-croatian
1.0 sec, instead they may fluctuate/vary from 0.5 sec up to 2.0 sec.	intervala između otkucaja, također poznatih kao R-R intervali.	english-croatian
	HRV označava fluktuacije otkucaja srca oko prosječnog broja otkucaja srca.	english-croatian
	Prosječan broj otkucaja srca	english-croatian
	od 60 otkucaja u minuti, ne znači da svi intervali između otkucaja u nizu traju točno 1 sekundu, nego oni	english-croatian
	mogu fluktuirati od 0,5 sek do 2 sek.	english-croatian
HRV is affected by aerobic fitness.	Na HRV utječe aerobna forma.	english-croatian
HRV of a well-conditioned heart is generally large at rest.	HRV srca u dobroj kondiciji, u mirovanju je općenito velik.	english-croatian
Other factors	Drugi čimbenici	english-croatian
that affect HRV are age, genetics, body position, time of day, and health status.	koji utječu na HRV su starost, genetika, položaj tijela, vrijeme dana i zdravlje.	english-croatian
During exercise, HRV	Tijekom vježbanja, HRV se	english-croatian
decreases as heart rate and exercise intensity increase.	smanjuje kako se povećava broj otkucaja srca i intenzitet vježbanja.	english-croatian
HRV also decreases during periods of mental	HRV se također smanjuje tijekom	english-croatian
stress.	razdoblja mentalnih napora.	english-croatian
HRV is regulated by the autonomic nervous system.	HRV-om upravlja automatski živčani sustav.	english-croatian
Parasympathetic activity decreases heart rate and	Para-suosjećajna aktivnost smanjuje broj otkucaja srca i	english-croatian
increases HRV, whereas sympathetic activity increases heart rate and decreases HRV.	povećava HRV, dok suosjećajna aktivnost povećava otkucaje srca i smanjuje HRV.	english-croatian
HRV is used in the Ownzone, OwnIndex, and in OwnOptimizer features.	HRV se koristi u Ownzone, OwnIndex i OwnOptimizer značajkama.	english-croatian

change in your training load and stress.	otkucaja srca, to može značiti promjenu u opterećenju vježbanja.	english-croatian
Running Cadence and Stride Length	Ritam trčanja i dužina koraka	english-croatian
Cadence* is the number of times the foot with the stride sensor* hits the ground per minute.	Ritam* je broj koraka stopala sa senzorom brzine trčanja* u minuti.	english-croatian
Stride length* is the average length of one step.	Dužina koraka* je prosječna dužina jednog koraka.	english-croatian
That is the distance between your right and left foot	To je udaljenost između desnog i lijevog stopala kad	english-croatian
contacting the ground.	dodirnu tlo.	english-croatian
Running speed = 2 * stride length * cadence	Brzina trčanja = 2 * dužina koraka * ritam	english-croatian
There are two ways to run faster: moving your legs at a higher cadence or taking longer steps.	Postoje dva načina za brže trčanje: pomicanje nogu s bržim ritmom ili uzimanje dužih koraka.	english-croatian
Elite long distance runners typically run with a high cadence of 85-95.	Elitni trkači na duge staze obično trče s visokim ritmom od 89-95.	english-croatian
On uphills, typical cadence values	Uzbrdo, uobičajene vrijednosti ritma su	english-croatian
are lower.	niže.	english-croatian
On downhills they are higher.	Nizbrdo, one su veće.	english-croatian
Runners adjust stride length to gather speed: stride length	Trkači namještaju dužinu koraka kako bi povećali brzinu: dužina koraka se	english-croatian
increases as speed increases.	povećava kako se povećava brzina.	english-croatian
Yet one of the most common mistakes novice runners make is over-striding.	Ipak, jedna od najčešćih pogrešaka koju čine novi trkači su preveliki koraci.	english-croatian
The most efficient stride	Najefikasnija dužina koraka	english-croatian
length is the natural one – the one that feels most comfortable.	je prirodna dužina – ona pri kojoj se osjećate najudobnije.	english-croatian
You will run faster in races by		english-croatian
strengthening your leg muscles so they take you forward with a longer stride.		english-croatian
You should also work on maximizing cadence efficiency.	U utrkama ćete trčati brže istezanjem mišića	english-croatian
Cadence does not progress easily, but if properly	nogu tako da vas odnesu dalje s dužim korakom.	english-croatian
trained, you will be able to sustain it throughout your runs and maximize your performance. To develop		english-croatian
cadence, the nerve-muscle connection needs to be trained - and reasonably frequently.		english-croatian
A session of cadence training a week is a good start.	Također bi trebali raditi na efikasnosti ritma.	english-croatian
Incorporate some cadence work into the rest of your week. During	Ritam se ne povećava lako, ali ako budete pravilno vježbali,	english-croatian
long easy runs, you could include some faster cadence every now and then.		english-croatian
When training for longer running events (½ Marathon, Marathon or longer), it may be helpful to monitor cadence.		english-croatian
A low cadence at expected race pace can cause problems later in the event, as your legs tire.		english-croatian
